## Research Report: Charlie Munger's Multidisciplinary Thinking Model

### **Charlie Munger and the Multidisciplinary Thinking Model**

Charlie Munger (1924-2023) was a renowned American investor, businessman, and philanthropist, best known for his long-term partnership with Warren Buffett as the Vice Chairman of Berkshire Hathaway [[1]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAKLjvICgvzYMPxvt_Mj8cW9bN4cX6NgpCLb9xPMLygZUctIUZgFj0NG6-OQeXeV4MCZsVyhRIX7xsdHnUp2vIMdYZ_sLjo0r7lP0RWaINZqlNCG9dZoxkyjCUhiJiL8YykOVRsip9CryuFPcg==)[[2]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAJgYmTmoqqo1XAMoxkiIvk-YbKHS4L9AwiEYR5c8ZnE7A7XIE6uLxFxuoia1zfFBCl0_lsF5NB_UrCON0jImbWJbjSypLiYphsk1nMFeI6GSqxEHIQpyN7o5uru_5fF2KJbXAe1N8v3vmltFDYDxIppr6K-NAHaOZk23lH_u7dUkq6rcdwTuCGY). Munger's investment philosophy and success were deeply rooted in his **multidisciplinary approach** to thinking [[3]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXGv0w970LpzkK9UUMMTmq9v0Fs5J1xcDJOsLrYwwwSTXBmxT-Zlar0oZzFtQSLmRLTFBcTuCU_Tk5BOcfCGnDAQPSRRfE7w4R_G013bwAxNwywlgX-7PaccxJKe8s-dpzBxaVhQF-ruW6gchNe0QTHghI0Dk08QYH5elfk-vg==)[[4]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXHcSTGOAV6ceJ9x7bwI8btxAf0izZGwviSoNqQm5GwdFyQvHbFzL6KPCH9PcXKKS4LsgyaJgJxOJ9FW7QvUJwItcsetBERbgDJ3BSZ_3YLUOaGCxj3RrQt8owe1-A2YXdbbrJY48RwWLMb5xiwivq87pPxrnyIHW2tRLQWCbpBgsPhaWg==)[[5]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAI5LGeNaQDpXPqGbKUF9A6W5iM7iDEGe7GJ72kUqNNdMnkBfsKho0dnIKDAhpXoA3NpXxxAGz9Y9l2LmREntV4orSConlPoMoRJUSKpZlRdX7pRYRWw8tH4LIUT475uIOux)[[6]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAL-BRklsGE62uLUxkzFV_uDCiIIEqFW0ddrETUxhNU-OFUE0rO6FFZFnvTqdhBFCkPRMO-P2hHdOHfS6StgNcArRu57cqGQaTHp2Tb1nVDIoBHmy9iUtbiLom1Crp-NYtNxGebslgqLNOVt2jEIO4kZsL9WPltFx3WekZP913UcSWMJrpfabB6UmfJJRv-cypD8U91c8e-tPdRVbzyQoXOeZKeaKXTRDwMm).

**Core Tenets of Munger's Investment Philosophy:**

Munger's approach is built upon several fundamental principles:

*   **Value Investing:** He sought to purchase businesses for less than their intrinsic value, a concept he refined from Benjamin Graham's teachings [[7]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAKu-mA-5Qb9GXZnlbXXj_H_K0sBkvQl6SbqaHcj3ht82phjX3gcxSL38qNa32YY4DaKGCrpJFOKSJXl1upsgEsSotWEJieEMRMov2PPeBL7Qj015rU8moyUsCutr3hBZJAfnlv1_6p7HSF4SjRw2_z50wYMmsICu3HrvT79cLCrfhLE8w==)[[8]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAKx-ZCkraECpw2zpP3qVl6zL_kCwoSRIIQms84mnJ3E49BeG-kOeopfxzDFZ40PiUAEn1cR5ZqNJ9j0Sby6BQSF68aP5at43eEUVsycOsxUjuZjKY0qNb0jonsJRHBaOY5t9QZqnZLEZ7YtQ1VrvJs55mRIbyoN4c_Ki4gsNpBGfKt8z43S)[[9]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAKXLueM8ZuT3A8vgRpHvN-PQexxg3Z1hpcB2BeeVLkmF5l6VWceGZ7cLE1xJ7fXMJ2S4YYYgcQUsJHPt4bKnbNmbOQuykdO62WHXejx96OuSLkxmb-TmiOjvf_Fjq5gF2YjRCOGBgTfxt79Tg-NSqtdvxjKYiVCixTdwmSzhALvj180UA==)[[10]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAL4h1eg_xU7z9SsgGdOEKHfYfhb1lTIeNW5VIv3V9tjonzP1xFlReHnWUOdiuof07adRUFx1QhBVOHBSHxi0v0KO97gdMqA4Vorfj37kZNU-NL72xgdIdGTyLI1paNP1z08MfiKdrJ9zJjVbUgtE-9ga4UEVZBj4dO0zJW7tpGkfNul)[[11]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAIrfisnt6tiuBPuAFEaLMyIQp9Ez9RsDoJ7ksty22GTAX77D4f0qW3G5TW4-eud40wL4QkK5kaiCMo9NJzOaksmGBWnBLCtPyTvVm3S6eiK9msp0amb0Ciak4pErlXM1mQ9tKLV7CwkyvXQ-ebkOKyuGsXlim2AxGgRYlBsg62pHvn5farocNgxBbRBhZYyTm0=). This involves a thorough understanding of a company's financials, competitive advantages, and long-term prospects to determine its true worth [[12]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXHZITiztt-MyYTU3qm3rwjAr1eHCrEwBkycdDMJJWBGdx4UDzhUdYYmpzjZsZ9zLgIndRRvcOTKtrHDVqkwMZ_V1Be3KmjHIk3TpK8lMbz77E9bHUut2Tcqp0FCyBe5-t6pakzBwFc-bQ6QtlyZzXW4lm3DGmiXPlKposy2dEhxMGofk_eAcbLQV5gPOqJk2S2iMvvES9hB)[[13]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXEjYQFogGVnsdwF0-iJTlQO73eDyGoLQiLi5pvw8YB-xAE2DlBmrlrf6YovitiyQOVAviGXyKEYVp5L77lVuayp2iGRtebAp6GaFFHYxzm_oqER0Iv0tb4RWYeQDx9EIJROkceoj5fkvfUuEw4AH9h-3QKgwBaCxSYJ4RNL7O_N8uudNU6_1KIcImzS5N6WH-T5178BGgU=)[[14]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAL4s9uHOwBA1TO4futw03DoWyp8cuwGsaf59ow_SN07euz5yHYyW_DNFxG7474-ZjNKwHA9AKD9hGAWGGmslmUDawuaUKalAoqMGfgkYbtqKorPeK_t8f0c4fYH6Bh5MTMg83gYQT7UZiwZ-gRveTMccPIXP0XXKyiphkKGplXQKOVAJk6ITG6heWWjcrfdOuS13uR1yjAKiA==).
*   **Quality Over Quantity:** Munger advocated for owning a small number of exceptional businesses rather than a large, diversified portfolio of mediocre ones [[15]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXHL8S41QFgf8_pe76SP8drdIGajJyFdmZdJrgMaGDWvwhoA_y6N0qTnfnyjOHIZuajvZECgRNtp-AUVCO_FSUdxVzzH2oGtw8W30zJvMDdh3LD3RTenWM83p83t8Jdi4HixHpeW-XRPjJe76r6EG2t_5zklaHs8OrhZa1W2SJQuzwFx0Ke4kB4=)[[16]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXF-ltZz9QW5DaMLuoPQUTM4jjEyylFb0PV0qeZq27kixsjRVl_7Isgc4hufjPKnkYtFIdoSBtnexbEVhqnahmC1oXYutVI1r4Q0Rzx_MlwXy3j024E1vOmhskUt5vWAhP1Rkn5ZJKh2RTVEj1BpXD1KIPyGpm_b93dktYL3bFIfmmCh8qPpyS3pbNd4iVXcFGc=)[[17]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXGMgMeXCWntpSKBaNMklmbCwYEim9e7zI95mKgFLSa52zi0BRpiXSPmCEaAyym7ZX-oVqPb6MFA7FNrgqPRlm44Ys-DfNPe86sNRrZvZOrH18QHGyfLJBSm1azToSW60vRo_m8l-hbcgSbKQVvKh2FOe6-gBbj_kMXsWptzXpi-J-SVABhLSUGsxq-Nhup17XIlH8kaT5xW)[[18]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXHpRoZBQClRwmJyxM9mCP-MReBmusPk5aYEgUhG2O5zat2OERJyjS1FdFCzrxIV4C75SDmisOKWdtrWk-PEoSgNuYb78_aJh7-samoGhaGYGa3XxPmYbHo-IQUY-wjHXpA0F7lukymcL_HNkB9BY8YFFIVFN2O8KaNAfmRsqRfp-f0zPJITbloR)[[12]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXHZITiztt-MyYTU3qm3rwjAr1eHCrEwBkycdDMJJWBGdx4UDzhUdYYmpzjZsZ9zLgIndRRvcOTKtrHDVqkwMZ_V1Be3KmjHIk3TpK8lMbz77E9bHUut2Tcqp0FCyBe5-t6pakzBwFc-bQ6QtlyZzXW4lm3DGmiXPlKposy2dEhxMGofk_eAcbLQV5gPOqJk2S2iMvvES9hB)[[19]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXFiPRZ7YoCZnyjlUteYCW3lqUxLcfVUHsbk6jxAYjmyXypK-rzOx0Vj7zLYhvLtFf19CU1FHlpzTmhSdJe-VDR2o9gTIO_Okueby04QnBXoUGclSrLI77xwXrCr0RGL4xRofF6tkGXH5txppiwHsx-0dSdU1mipmsBcVWjGzhGfPzORnMa7TXA=)[[20]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAK6ezQT-cE8r6mrArS9j91PAgu6wn_TX7xMG11JpvTlbV-uXmUlWIT4tb34iCyMsEDb9b87lA7WtENl-v6rHYcbRr--Z4tTPs40WxxizvyiPA0LkVzrSQmXw6DCdhMcKXBxYnjWrUa3K12oa7Mo2Xp3K43yFRPzCE_4RDUPG06IHreqqQhWhYh-fjC22_su8MK4F17dyFlghNIocMmL)[[21]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAJcZtdyc1dKggjpQgtEAMo07KKlrHCwV *   **Constant Learning and Preparation:** Superior performance stems from a constant search for better thought methods, rigorous preparation, and multidisciplinary research [[42]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXH4eSvO5zN08SeZts2cpASqbVAeGWsEnSIlOsW2K4UpQiC31v-R9gM2_C2pP5ReWnmp9f-iIBLH2ngt4HKOP41xM72_YNSSIAPMqEsrm4l14hp7lnkphDN6e6ddFc3Bqe9lF7q95VcySrBfXvf5KyWMFbOlO22c1VdAzlP3H-f3W4td6gWWzArXdvVvgXiUS_MPyJVyda8MtJ2e)[[44]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXEysQBUcI4ZWm9eSH0L24yq2XJWwdzUnzHoQuKz3zzAbS3SLDwXmYm7ZSg6HXA0198CnCyIZAEXfRvphefnH0Si50BftVUiHExnVr81LVPsaHwT8Xkf-tDN2qLIiphrGbYvx90_sMErZm-Io7VEiH9daYcptahwj42jLsPYu4kAmxz8kpBoYvAhA-Whfn0-WW6d6_OdrL93ZiF1)[[60]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAIX62hcCZOeJjn3tb0HYJR-azF_YKqKv_I72Rt8H4be3yc-sdTuf4z_Q7WBWdqVKinHDtpm4m1fNddiugueBNp_qtVOpiev6enQj4iaUgcfhBMbr_2bDX6PrxUh6hxQeZ4VDwsyk_FwCdeZUqzcNoE-_KP2hthNdy30Wlnga3IZ-op8OpDVzJVKpSnhiTFM88mPZMGfvaLeavXi3g==)[[49]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAIj8PdskszIMCy7ScxizjxlZ9w-fRHAvVCvQjHVkOIeZ5qkUZ4oxAtX_IDaOqg2auqiM714adoW2XPzkqLAucBu4cp-oqk4ZRei3rLZ7E1L48fy4GevMZjv92zERzyoTrSTLRs34pC3TXH2fOzxRBsrcc1gp4TRuRIOHKG4mE2XWcV8BGClgNeMRXEh-fnwOlDtQO8TQ3Ss-NKH3g==).

**Multidisciplinary Thinking Model:**

Munger's multidisciplinary approach involves integrating knowledge from diverse fields to form a comprehensive understanding of complex situations [[3]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXGv0w970LpzkK9UUMMTmq9v0Fs5J1xcDJOsLrYwwwSTXBmxT-Zlar0oZzFtQSLmRLTFBcTuCU_Tk5BOcfCGnDAQPSRRfE7w4R_G013bwAxNwywlgX-7PaccxJKe8s-dpzBxaVhQF-ruW6gchNe0QTHghI0Dk08QYH5elfk-vg==)[[4]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXHcSTGOAV6ceJ9x7bwI8btxAf0izZGwviSoNqQm5GwdFyQvHbFzL6KPCH9PcXKKS4LsgyaJgJxOJ9FW7QvUJwItcsetBERbgDJ3BSZ_3YLUOaGCxj3RrQt8owe1-A2YXdbbrJY48RwWLMb5xiwivq87pPxrnyIHW2tRLQWCbpBgsPhaWg==)[[35]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqALm3LvKRZxYr2XgqdOI45JomLKI9vlSR2YNGmCsQggWSspU7HxbtW6Jr3BTeWL3jMevGPZOwVK8Sc_aP8MsJABiGnX5uplIg_yNmgeTsu74WGaJ6q0n64OJ62ombWg3xKrVWPPg4_2PMhQ7L1fRvB1WcKWbiQHFpVB-nLLeodHf2davuUX93WLS_-RslSupsX9iHeS5jcmiojetiup42iedmznHWC9y_d9c)[[36]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAL7J4VY2D7JwYP_V9SjPU3qOoT740SfSBpNqNOV0Mx62Ivcy_NBiiXMZvc2UudVN46e1sPlIkeBvsx9G3WbV25_OsEQLOVlhwyj8QHcwLAjbtFZKznowvrZaxTa62JzGWxUY4gee_I=)[[37]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAJ0jl4WCKetuobCBzsNZsxxL-xOYgPqrbaDTxfVm9nZdmK3ZqntnV3-Wgqb1i0ME49U_L6tf__6xf4Dwfn5KAonLUPNRwmZqp0jmIll4eSREBV-gcrKwtJOTeb5pz2-61cRFIqhDPKVVYoKUUU7zH1rUhLGBnfoLA55BmWqgPs85HB-meWuccGzgg==)[[5]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAI5LGeNaQDpXPqGbKUF9A6W5iM7iDEGe7GJ72kUqNNdMnkBfsKho0dnIKDAhpXoA3NpXxxAGz9Y9l2LmREntV4orSConlPoMoRJUSKpZlRdX7pRYRWw8tH4LIUT475uIOux)[[6]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAL-BRklsGE62uLUxkzFV_uDCiIIEqFW0ddrETUxhNU-OFUE0rO6FFZFnvTqdhBFCkPRMO-P2hHdOHfS6StgNcArRu57cqGQaTHp2Tb1nVDIoBHmy9iUtbiLom1Crp-NYtNxGebslgqLNOVt2jEIO4kZsL9WPltFx3WekZP913UcSWMJrpfabB6UmfJJRv-cypD8U91c8e-tPdRVbzyQoXOeZKeaKXTRDwMm)[[38]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqALGtD3vTRxpL0lUM3SLyIyZehx3ivYu8A2U1kCqD8zmzT--Z_02mnspQ-Ub2B24Hzd0_fJZhqWaI8U6GdRESdT4t-z9Bl8eUO33WhencTU9ihtXjLi4Z5jjIUgq-IyeWEthYVdTF0k=)[[39]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAIStEqI4zqTHOgo47nGPsnxBEJ5SuNf9BAnt7OODdqY6TEFJF3Kq5BQ8rP3BNgeRMD-GU8Ke996j6eWWo_JykO7EuKoKdNVWUh4gVML-XaBXGsfUNXXLLrwzHWb2R-Meny5uP6HNg-tTwBqEW05m6b28vLHxk7rn80Pe2p2x1-uYlmWvFt1rECbaG_kfEHGAdXFFfoguWeSSNwgOAYqx1chdkuNTmfNyk8T)[[40]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAJq00KFaR2Sg3fQhopUOBAOgC_h7nyCfvKVQAStbHloIVn2GM1Fdx28OJmO23vK57lV_H4KLLIkqc5Z82WmT4gHndljffLTywmwANWvqB2_Q59L1U7MbOEr0pxo92WCwDKWciVDcuM=)[[41]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAJuLqwcOUC48mJKpQPaR4tUjdvLVVA9RS_2m57nq4v3vmMYH8sEWMExwSHjXnYOwomd-su2fNcWc2OP4Iq0pE3uhWf8dYqraOXF2k7sdIeX7aj_N88ZlcA_E-PI940LI0Mlxo1I7FARGn2MZJ64L6zww07numzAOKwpn-0R4kN9NaJ2lsvHzlgxvA==). He used **mental models**, cognitive frameworks from various disciplines, to view problems from multiple perspectives. His favorite models included inversion, circle of competence, and a latticework of mental models [[3]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXGv0w970LpzkK9UUMMTmq9v0Fs5J1xcDJOsLrYwwwSTXBmxT-Zlar0oZzFtQSLmRLTFBcTuCU_Tk5BOcfCGnDAQPSRRfE7w4R_G013bwAxNwywlgX-7PaccxJKe8s-dpzBxaVhQF-ruW6gchNe0QTHghI0Dk08QYH5elfk-vg==).

### **Psychological Thinking Models**

Understanding human psychology is crucial for investors, as cognitive biases can significantly impair decision-making [[67]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXHqMCEGEDoiCnoLuRcyTvW0AIziEUw9OEc5IL2KWjUDUCJ1EMKfNU0nTqs6H3av2jf5rDHbHMa7fLebEt1JHSQVeU-SCMmnZG3XVkvf9BhEkQTPcNOA1nTjpxD5vkDXWJ-fEJUwLVwxIdbmELvDzOYcm4pPXy-MAJLan10n7Xo9bz6YwdmLmKrALHlrgBAhKUtR9BroVs2iRoK3Q8Y3IWrQK3hTLEpqeg==)[[68]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXGGwX_ef8MoBDloO0YJOglB10VJMVnI-w7SzeXtlQD9Du16U56Aw9wog7AGyH5uTOCZvI0s0V1YfAMZxZ6kbrcP1tlreTqAdHdYoliVg0q1OT-_sXIgzgpWDeWR9vvRyAd2yxYQ_fV6Hjjv09mKkkA_iDihhAbRkPYa7eCL_OE5aSc=)[[69]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAIqIUU2_TbJVZj9UwV6AdNR6QA8319E183beIDG8ho_jSnyRYV_tzsiESaOdK5eO2alkCgfYMdFdshhJ8Y_vlPqab-yA7l80xIkQLl8lqrgqgWOQQ80nxBzI4uOMSTDWMpsB3nbRitnFD1eOR5ylGrbDBC86N_L18heySsY3YYHf0ESN_lAxzUVKQ==). Munger emphasized rationality and avoiding these biases [[53]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXH_KE10fzi6nB7-IUIWAdcK4jd5jWIlFvjIScQ8IPsevQ4IAa6pOGsd2k03C7x7ycGrhG0C8YRJPXY-GDb6BMRfJv89RbXjGJvmt2LN_C5nP3CXd8tmHmGzzd1PIvJWyTfonl0etS5UWdQ5rtskfXWelauxZ5QLUBJOterwT5D2R8b9HtcWIdwK6tmjISUY7Z9CHyz20BbMkp3QbY2WgHem6Zox6rZuqvim-ViqiWD3ptcByffGXNXlxBw95KNu663rdvKKk0U6zRiHhqBZjPRwgi1FdVyFzU86mAI-5wPx2MlHhMbe5tD74uKubuw9)[[67]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXHqMCEGEDoiCnoLuRcyTvW0AIziEUw9OEc5IL2KWjUDUCJ1EMKfNU0nTqs6H3av2jf5rDHbHMa7fLebEt1JHSQVeU-SCMmnZG3XVkvf9BhEkQTPcNOA1nTjpxD5vkDXWJ-fEJUwLVwxIdbmELvDzOYcm4pPXy-MAJLan10n7Xo9bz6YwdmLmKrALHlrgBAhKUtR9BroVs2iRoK3Q8Y3IWrQK3hTLEpqeg==)[[68]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXGGwX_ef8MoBDloO0YJOglB10VJMVnI-w7SzeXtlQD9Du16U56Aw9wog7AGyH5uTOCZvI0s0V1YfAMZxZ6kbrcP1tlreTqAdHdYoliVg0q1OT-_sXIgzgpWDeWR9vvRyAd2yxYQ_fV6Hjjv09mKkkA_iDihhAbRkPYa7eCL_OE5aSc=)[[70]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXGfziUIX8JYzrOJzvDotHeq2p5Io8uJ1hDayKLLolcD57vWjCqTppYvHKzCSya2-IP5bWufIlL6oF10M7AXgWSDppg0kisA1DeFWEAJ34Ebai7feaOidSYrJNQm5CX-CtJGQHFO_nFJ)[[71]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXGttN_MYIYDQG-ATFlgNxyxOCJRLJAxqsCtFApi-16sfzUktmrd_zsKOKLscJBjw91cICbkeQdpq6mx1IHPejEo9SzjW_9y7mawTtwlnnjPkIaE4QQtEylQGv8aB1XqVyUVJmJ1W8DTNIjGfcg4YnaigDW0dReZ3kBHjUu3khtOJCZNUSU7PHYmxagpwcY_XEE-curR3DL_3fXXNCRRdr1st5zId9uJOlnLuzh112G2yRojfQ==)[[72]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXGOueszJgA8jXmOwtrO27U72jj35WxnZaXUKiwJs4WTDI-a_6ZAJGwEE_mPEV223jOjRJLMN6YvFhUhYSDgnHKyHbnit4t4RrOQs0YQ5mG8COcDEYO9iU6HSOp1flxJkmqulQUJ-rfXD29Uxr4qkzNiGJe-6J4WSI9lfjC-8L1kRg3icCat7l1ZuDy_sSwO4_hPb59guKBHrv620tgJx-QCFzyThba9Tm0yC8kCGyKy)[[3]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXGv0w970LpzkK9UUMMTmq9v0Fs5J1xcDJOsLrYwwwSTXBmxT-Zlar0oZzFtQSLmRLTFBcTuCU_Tk5BOcfCGnDAQPSRRfE7w4R_G013bwAxNwywlgX-7PaccxJKe8s-dpzBxaVhQF-ruW6gchNe0QTHghI0Dk08QYH5elfk-vg==)[[37]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAJ0jl4WCKetuobCBzsNZsxxL-xOYgPqrbaDTxfVm9nZdmK3ZqntnV3-Wgqb1i0ME49U_L6tf__6xf4Dwfn5KAonLUPNRwmZqp0jmIll4eSREBV-gcrKwtJOTeb5pz2-61cRFIqhDPKVVYoKUUU7zH1rUhLGBnfoLA55BmWqgPs85HB-meWuccGzgg==)[[69]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAIqIUU2_TbJVZj9UwV6AdNR6QA8319E183beIDG8ho_jSnyRYV_tzsiESaOdK5eO2alkCgfYMdFdshhJ8Y_vlPqab-yA7l80xIkQLl8lqrgqgWOQQ80nxBzI4uOMSTDWMpsB3nbRitnFD1eOR5ylGrbDBC86N_L18heySsY3YYHf0ESN_lAxzUVKQ==).

**Examples of Relevant Cognitive Biases:**

*   **Anchoring Bias:** Over-relying on the first piece of information received (the "anchor") when making decisions, even if irrelevant.
*   **Availability Heuristic:** Overestimating the importance of information easily available or recalled, like recent news [[68]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXGGwX_ef8MoBDloO0YJOglB10VJMVnI-w7SzeXtlQD9Du16U56Aw9wog7AGyH5uTOCZvI0s0V1YfAMZxZ6kbrcP1tlreTqAdHdYoliVg0q1OT-_sXIgzgpWDeWR9vvRyAd2yxYQ_fV6Hjjv09mKkkA_iDihhAbRkPYa7eCL_OE5aSc=).
*   **Confirmation Bias:** Seeking out and interpreting information that confirms existing beliefs, ignoring contradictory evidence [[67]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXHqMCEGEDoiCnoLuRcyTvW0AIziEUw9OEc5IL2KWjUDUCJ1EMKfNU0nTqs6H3av2jf5rDHbHMa7fLebEt1JHSQVeU-SCMmnZG3XVkvf9BhEkQTPcNOA1nTjpxD5vkDXWJ-fEJUwLVwxIdbmELvDzOYcm4pPXy-MAJLan10n7Xo9bz6YwdmLmKrALHlrgBAhKUtR9BroVs2iRoK3Q8Y3IWrQK3hTLEpqeg==)[[70]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXGfziUIX8JYzrOJzvDotHeq2p5Io8uJ1hDayKLLolcD57vWjCqTppYvHKzCSya2-IP5bWufIlL6oF10M7AXgWSDppg0kisA1DeFWEAJ34Ebai7feaOidSYrJNQm5CX-CtJGQHFO_nFJ)[[71]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXGttN_MYIYDQG-ATFlgNxyxOCJRLJAxqsCtFApi-16sfzUktmrd_zsKOKLscJBjw91cICbkeQdpq6mx1IHPejEo9SzjW_9y7mawTtwlnnjPkIaE4QQtEylQGv8aB1XqVyUVJmJ1W8DTNIjGfcg4YnaigDW0dReZ3kBHjUu3khtOJCZNUSU7PHYmxagpwcY_XEE-curR3DL_3fXXNCRRdr1st5zId9uJOlnLuzh112G2yRojfQ==).
*   **Endowment Effect:** Overvaluing assets simply because they are owned [[67]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXHqMCEGEDoiCnoLuRcyTvW0AIziEUw9OEc5IL2KWjUDUCJ1EMKfNU0nTqs6H3av2jf5rDHbHMa7fLebEt1JHSQVeU-SCMmnZG3XVkvf9BhEkQTPcNOA1nTjpxD5vkDXWJ-fEJUwLVwxIdbmELvDzOYcm4pPXy-MAJLan10n7Xo9bz6YwdmLmKrALHlrgBAhKUtR9BroVs2iRoK3Q8Y3IWrQK3hTLEpqeg==)[[70]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXGfziUIX8JYzrOJzvDotHeq2p5Io8uJ1hDayKLLolcD57vWjCqTppYvHKzCSya2-IP5bWufIlL6oF10M7AXgWSDppg0kisA1DeFWEAJ34Ebai7feaOidSYrJNQm5CX-CtJGQHFO_nFJ).
*   **Hindsight Bias:** Believing, after an event, that one could have predicted it, leading to overconfidence [[72]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXGOueszJgA8jXmOwtrO27U72jj35WxnZaXUKiwJs4WTDI-a_6ZAJGwEE_mPEV223jOjRJLMN6YvFhUhYSDgnHKyHbnit4t4RrOQs0YQ5mG8COcDEYO9iU6HSOp1flxJkmqulQUJ-rfXD29Uxr4qkzNiGJe-6J4WSI9lfjC-8L1kRg3icCat7l1ZuDy_sSwO4_hPb59guKBHrv620tgJx-QCFzyThba9Tm0yC8kCGyKy).
*   **Illusion of Control Bias:** Overestimating one's ability to influence investment outcomes [[70]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXGfziUIX8JYzrOJzvDotHeq2p5Io8uJ1hDayKLLolcD57vWjCqTppYvHKzCSya2-IP5bWufIlL6oF10M7AXgWSDppg0kisA1DeFWEAJ34Ebai7feaOidSYrJNQm5CX-CtJGQHFO_nFJ).
*   **Information Bias:** Making decisions based on irrelevant information [[72]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXGOueszJgA8jXmOwtrO27U72jj35WxnZaXUKiwJs4WTDI-a_6ZAJGwEE_mPEV223jOjRJLMN6YvFhUhYSDgnHKyHbnit4t4RrOQs0YQ5mG8COcDEYO9iU6HSOp1flxJkmqulQUJ-rfXD29Uxr4qkzNiGJe-6J4WSI9lfjC-8L1kRg3icCat7l1ZuDy_sSwO4_hPb59guKBHrv620tgJx-QCFzyThba9Tm0yC8kCGyKy).
*   **Loss Aversion:** Feeling the pain of a loss more strongly than the pleasure of an equivalent gain [[67]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXHqMCEGEDoiCnoLuRcyTvW0AIziEUw9OEc5IL2KWjUDUCJ1EMKfNU0nTqs6H3av2jf5rDHbHMa7fLebEt1JHSQVeU-SCMmnZG3XVkvf9BhEkQTPcNOA1nTjpxD5vkDXWJ-fEJUwLVwxIdbmELvDzOYcm4pPXy-MAJLan10n7Xo9bz6YwdmLmKrALHlrgBAhKUtR9BroVs2iRoK3Q8Y3IWrQK3hTLEpqeg==)[[68]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXGGwX_ef8MoBDloO0YJOglB10VJMVnI-w7SzeXtlQD9Du16U56Aw9wog7AGyH5uTOCZvI0s0V1YfAMZxZ6kbrcP1tlreTqAdHdYoliVg0q1OT-_sXIgzgpWDeWR9vvRyAd2yxYQ_fV6Hjjv09mKkkA_iDihhAbRkPYa7eCL_OE5aSc=)[[71]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXGttN_MYIYDQG-ATFlgNxyxOCJRLJAxqsCtFApi-16sfzUktmrd_zsKOKLscJBjw91cICbkeQdpq6mx1IHPejEo9SzjW_9y7mawTtwlnnjPkIaE4QQtEylQGv8aB1XqVyUVJmJ1W8DTNIjGfcg4YnaigDW0dReZ3kBHjUu3khtOJCZNUSU7PHYmxagpwcY_XEE-curR3DL_3fXXNCRRdr1st5zId9uJOlnLuzh112G2yRojfQ==)[[72]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXGOueszJgA8jXmOwtrO27U72jj35WxnZaXUKiwJs4WTDI-a_6ZAJGwEE_mPEV223jOjRJLMN6YvFhUhYSDgnHKyHbnit4t4RrOQs0YQ5mG8COcDEYO9iU6HSOp1flxJkmqulQUJ-rfXD29Uxr4qkzNiGJe-6J4WSI9lfjC-8L1kRg3icCat7l1ZuDy_sSwO4_hPb59guKBHrv620tgJx-QCFzyThba9Tm0yC8kCGyKy).
*   **Overconfidence Bias:** Overestimating one's own knowledge and abilities [[67]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXHqMCEGEDoiCnoLuRcyTvW0AIziEUw9OEc5IL2KWjUDUCJ1EMKfNU0nTqs6H3av2jf5rDHbHMa7fLebEt1JHSQVeU-SCMmnZG3XVkvf9BhEkQTPcNOA1nTjpxD5vkDXWJ-fEJUwLVwxIdbmELvDzOYcm4pPXy-MAJLan10n7Xo9bz6YwdmLmKrALHlrgBAhKUtR9BroVs2iRoK3Q8Y3IWrQK3hTLEpqeg==)[[70]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXGfziUIX8JYzrOJzvDotHeq2p5Io8uJ1hDayKLLolcD57vWjCqTppYvHKzCSya2-IP5bWufIlL6oF10M7AXgWSDppg0kisA1DeFWEAJ34Ebai7feaOidSYrJNQm5CX-CtJGQHFO_nFJ).
*   **Oversimplification Tendency:** Making poor decisions by oversimplifying complex situations [[72]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXGOueszJgA8jXmOwtrO27U72jj35WxnZaXUKiwJs4WTDI-a_6ZAJGwEE_mPEV223jOjRJLMN6YvFhUhYSDgnHKyHbnit4t4RrOQs0YQ5mG8COcDEYO9iU6HSOp1flxJkmqulQUJ-rfXD29Uxr4qkzNiGJe-6J4WSI9lfjC-8L1kRg3icCat7l1ZuDy_sSwO4_hPb59guKBHrv620tgJx-QCFzyThba9Tm0yC8kCGyKy).
*   **Regret Aversion:** Avoiding decisions that could lead to regret, even if beneficial [[71]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXGttN_MYIYDQG-ATFlgNxyxOCJRLJAxqsCtFApi-16sfzUktmrd_zsKOKLscJBjw91cICbkeQdpq6mx1IHPejEo9SzjW_9y7mawTtwlnnjPkIaE4QQtEylQGv8aB1XqVyUVJmJ1W8DTNIjGfcg4YnaigDW0dReZ3kBHjUu3khtOJCZNUSU7PHYmxagpwcY_XEE-curR3DL_3fXXNCRRdr1st5zId9uJOlnLuzh112G2yRojfQ==).
*   **Status Quo Bias:** Preferring the current situation, even when change is necessary [[68]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXGGwX_ef8MoBDloO0YJOglB10VJMVnI-w7SzeXtlQD9Du16U56Aw9wog7AGyH5uTOCZvI0s0V1YfAMZxZ6kbrcP1tlreTqAdHdYoliVg0q1OT-_sXIgzgpWDeWR9vvRyAd2yxYQ_fV6Hjjv09mKkkA_iDihhAbRkPYa7eCL_OE5aSc=)[[70]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXGfziUIX8JYzrOJzvDotHeq2p5Io8uJ1hDayKLLolcD57vWjCqTppYvHKzCSya2-IP5bWufIlL6oF10M7AXgWSDppg0kisA1DeFWEAJ34Ebai7feaOidSYrJNQm5CX-CtJGQHFO_nFJ).
*   **Herding Bias:** Following the crowd, even against one's own analysis [[67]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXHqMCEGEDoiCnoLuRcyTvW0AIziEUw9OEc5IL2KWjUDUCJ1EMKfNU0nTqs6H3av2jf5rDHbHMa7fLebEt1JHSQVeU-SCMmnZG3XVkvf9BhEkQTPcNOA1nTjpxD5vkDXWJ-fEJUwLVwxIdbmELvDzOYcm4pPXy-MAJLan10n7Xo9bz6YwdmLmKrALHlrgBAhKUtR9BroVs2iRoK3Q8Y3IWrQK3hTLEpqeg==).

### **Mathematical Thinking Models**

Mathematics provides tools for analyzing data, assessing probabilities, and understanding growth [[3]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXGv0w970LpzkK9UUMMTmq9v0Fs5J1xcDJOsLrYwwwSTXBmxT-Zlar0oZzFtQSLmRLTFBcTuCU_Tk5BOcfCGnDAQPSRRfE7w4R_G013bwAxNwywlgX-7PaccxJKe8s-dpzBxaVhQF-ruW6gchNe0QTHghI0Dk08QYH5elfk-vg==)[[73]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXEu0WQIwzUkWaPw9lFPxAyNPLT1gEIUf-acJ2smYVCVBk7_9hZF24tYuFMzq2x_4r1cWkkoL4aBWqNocSUk2JQsYrJy7-7Fl6y79lV6zrhRMZQgsUdsmdTKUH8JPZ2vFq4u4j_9wo_3fBzk2LPngMD7HNzq0CMoK1clsa5LvfnWzOQWTUQVYkgfZYlLiFwxwUplmVoQzo2MsMgCt2UdELxSGSVE3lkWAho=)[[74]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXEtBuG42K_2YYpnadtnUtWDbP7UetCZQCP_VObbR8FsZsZV2FLQIiY8IQd49Aq52gkwlMn2gtQtjKZm0QGU3VN_isqiaYf49Kh_5jBk9dvmXE3ierdONJ4rr38aG-OF6c7wlilFYHCqZc-h1XbgtKHdK1-h3RTqO1NWs5rFGPikXl5Uijg=)[[75]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXFs0ylx1kfsAlcAHYBcVa2vu-rXR1SZOwrL_Yh10_rQXnH4mfKajKcuo0jFY7tjWFvjrd6hZYTPFvLwzgWdZYitZP40YF3gkWpusww1RDj7xg0OZGerF61tV7WKpO-hpAO-o9LSoqWS2y8Hzc1GmunMneHzvrZSFuTVt58StcWpTx0u-Q==)[[76]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXENf8Iub5t5tqoEafW3AJDFo0FTyvsYl2VeSjD_6-4M357TgV4a6dArt78ijeGabgqSSROuzR1d8o7_Wl5C_kvPh6M0eiHUPoOkVZkvbO07M4AENEofPFoZJJULOPFUGHHGf973fc8Y3qrOkXQzkv9qGq9ItzvmTL4=)[[77]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAJHzi3d9QsYRWZsigYLpl25OJEEMgADDcU_b7D6qTbVTcQ8qx9kvY2j4ISmFM1dsX5E0N2XlEeFcsj9N-R8VgGvv74VOnPqt11_CwPiM_VPle2oNJR0JaxymkpAgh2KvBMijFlwTeHAB3oCPFnpf0BuNd_xp3-ZQBd5XcHHFFf7E9tbS-0=)[[78]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAKDVA2G2zcGsY5kRWj2WU0-Sa7HUSCKpTfE0TggJsL8-_fGXRQZ5eFhm4lPbO9fz-lSmli3zFW7BG1pu9rjtSsK04cK9f4jvcNqHl9UbR_2RaE9L-tMdcdrRySw-UTIp5rat3_o04nP3Jq7SZf4r2ptT06ipueyPyHE6hPQG7QuGNwGHg==).

**Examples of Mathematical Models Used in Investment Analysis:**

*   **Probability Theory:** Understanding probabilities is fundamental for risk assessment [[3]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXGv0w970LpzkK9UUMMTmq9v0Fs5J1xcDJOsLrYwwwSTXBmxT-Zlar0oZzFtQSLmRLTFBcTuCU_Tk5BOcfCGnDAQPSRRfE7w4R_G013bwAxNwywlgX-7PaccxJKe8s-dpzBxaVhQF-ruW6gchNe0QTHghI0Dk08QYH5elfk-vg==).
*   **Statistics:** Regression analysis, time series analysis (e.g., ARIMA), and sampling theory are used for forecasting and data analysis [[76]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXENf8Iub5t5tqoEafW3AJDFo0FTyvsYl2VeSjD_6-4M357TgV4a6dArt78ijeGabgqSSROuzR1d8o7_Wl5C_kvPh6M0eiHUPoOkVZkvbO07M4AENEofPFoZJJULOPFUGHHGf973fc8Y3qrOkXQzkv9qGq9ItzvmTL4=)[[78]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAKDVA2G2zcGsY5kRWj2WU0-Sa7HUSCKpTfE0TggJsL8-_fGXRQZ5eFhm4lPbO9fz-lSmli3zFW7BG1pu9rjtSsK04cK9f4jvcNqHl9UbR_2RaE9L-tMdcdrRySw-UTIp5rat3_o04nP3Jq7SZf4r2ptT06ipueyPyHE6hPQG7QuGNwGHg==).
*   **Compound Interest:** Munger called it the "eighth wonder of the world," highlighting its power in long-term investing [[57]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAJEqWlIx_K-A5yclorW4lcPOyvZNErVSNqSIpjJgBfPiVZoMhg67-oMkvLjYgGeSNP53Ns5gBSXnDvrr7FBtkyOq9i7TTcZkjpvZmtdDeWDqzbEa20IqRlPNMX9B3MVnr7pr_1qrTCLX8JUAYhsbl--MeeDhHyMZB7_EDiqzwtSdJuBAPoB5gJU8OyrAESZ1RM4X_2qspnAleYuFFYfXoV7WX490GwDBtlIWeQwoJjSYN6MRiQ5G_B9_xTKe2Ea0pRY_llaEA==)[[31]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAKorpJiCPcKnKTPUmfgXDmPLUYziVhVNmP8556YCzz1mCH59klRCRo0o3oyuzDhktT2roF6piBehBLVkvlLdYRkU5U0CbN2CdSO6n3aou4IhHks88TsgVjh5uBFxGGYD8WZut87LByGdZhjVMSwCNfBAaU8CFg2uFMn9il_dQnd59Or93QPyVyo).
*   **Capital Asset Pricing Model (CAPM):** Used to determine the expected return on an asset based on its risk [[74]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXEtBuG42K_2YYpnadtnUtWDbP7UetCZQCP_VObbR8FsZsZV2FLQIiY8IQd49Aq52gkwlMn2gtQtjKZm0QGU3VN_isqiaYf49Kh_5jBk9dvmXE3ierdONJ4rr38aG-OF6c7wlilFYHCqZc-h1XbgtKHdK1-h3RTqO1NWs5rFGPikXl5Uijg=)[[77]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAJHzi3d9QsYRWZsigYLpl25OJEEMgADDcU_b7D6qTbVTcQ8qx9kvY2j4ISmFM1dsX5E0N2XlEeFcsj9N-R8VgGvv74VOnPqt11_CwPiM_VPle2oNJR0JaxymkpAgh2KvBMijFlwTeHAB3oCPFnpf0BuNd_xp3-ZQBd5XcHHFFf7E9tbS-0=).
*   **Arbitrage Pricing Theory (APT):** A multifactor model using macroeconomic factors to predict returns [[74]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXEtBuG42K_2YYpnadtnUtWDbP7UetCZQCP_VObbR8FsZsZV2FLQIiY8IQd49Aq52gkwlMn2gtQtjKZm0QGU3VN_isqiaYf49Kh_5jBk9dvmXE3ierdONJ4rr38aG-OF6c7wlilFYHCqZc-h1XbgtKHdK1-h3RTqO1NWs5rFGPikXl5Uijg=).
*   **Black-Scholes Model:** Used to estimate the price of European-style options [[73]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXEu0WQIwzUkWaPw9lFPxAyNPLT1gEIUf-acJ2smYVCVBk7_9hZF24tYuFMzq2x_4r1cWkkoL4aBWqNocSUk2JQsYrJy7-7Fl6y79lV6zrhRMZQgsUdsmdTKUH8JPZ2vFq4u4j_9wo_3fBzk2LPngMD7HNzq0CMoK1clsa5LvfnWzOQWTUQVYkgfZYlLiFwxwUplmVoQzo2MsMgCt2UdELxSGSVE3lkWAho=)[[76]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXENf8Iub5t5tqoEafW3AJDFo0FTyvsYl2VeSjD_6-4M357TgV4a6dArt78ijeGabgqSSROuzR1d8o7_Wl5C_kvPh6M0eiHUPoOkVZkvbO07M4AENEofPFoZJJULOPFUGHHGf973fc8Y3qrOkXQzkv9qGq9ItzvmTL4=).
*   **Monte Carlo Simulation:** Uses random sampling to model the probability of different outcomes [[73]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXEu0WQIwzUkWaPw9lFPxAyNPLT1gEIUf-acJ2smYVCVBk7_9hZF24tYuFMzq2x_4r1cWkkoL4aBWqNocSUk2JQsYrJy7-7Fl6y79lV6zrhRMZQgsUdsmdTKUH8JPZ2vFq4u4j_9wo_3fBzk2LPngMD7HNzq0CMoK1clsa5LvfnWzOQWTUQVYkgfZYlLiFwxwUplmVoQzo2MsMgCt2UdELxSGSVE3lkWAho=)[[74]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXEtBuG42K_2YYpnadtnUtWDbP7UetCZQCP_VObbR8FsZsZV2FLQIiY8IQd49Aq52gkwlMn2gtQtjKZm0QGU3VN_isqiaYf49Kh_5jBk9dvmXE3ierdONJ4rr38aG-OF6c7wlilFYHCqZc-h1XbgtKHdK1-h3RTqO1NWs5rFGPikXl5Uijg=).
*   **Value-at-Risk (VaR) Models:** Quantify potential losses associated with financial positions [[73]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXEu0WQIwzUkWaPw9lFPxAyNPLT1gEIUf-acJ2smYVCVBk7_9hZF24tYuFMzq2x_4r1cWkkoL4aBWqNocSUk2JQsYrJy7-7Fl6y79lV6zrhRMZQgsUdsmdTKUH8JPZ2vFq4u4j_9wo_3fBzk2LPngMD7HNzq0CMoK1clsa5LvfnWzOQWTUQVYkgfZYlLiFwxwUplmVoQzo2MsMgCt2UdELxSGSVE3lkWAho=)[[75]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXFs0ylx1kfsAlcAHYBcVa2vu-rXR1SZOwrL_Yh10_rQXnH4mfKajKcuo0jFY7tjWFvjrd6hZYTPFvLwzgWdZYitZP40YF3gkWpusww1RDj7xg0OZGerF61tV7WKpO-hpAO-o9LSoqWS2y8Hzc1GmunMneHzvrZSFuTVt58StcWpTx0u-Q==)[[78]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAKDVA2G2zcGsY5kRWj2WU0-Sa7HUSCKpTfE0TggJsL8-_fGXRQZ5eFhm4lPbO9fz-lSmli3zFW7BG1pu9rjtSsK04cK9f4jvcNqHl9UbR_2RaE9L-tMdcdrRySw-UTIp5rat3_o04nP3Jq7SZf4r2ptT06ipueyPyHE6hPQG7QuGNwGHg==).
*   **Economic Value Added (EVA) Valuation Model:** An investment value analysis method [[74]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXEtBuG42K_2YYpnadtnUtWDbP7UetCZQCP_VObbR8FsZsZV2FLQIiY8IQd49Aq52gkwlMn2gtQtjKZm0QGU3VN_isqiaYf49Kh_5jBk9dvmXE3ierdONJ4rr38aG-OF6c7wlilFYHCqZc-h1XbgtKHdK1-h3RTqO1NWs5rFGPikXl5Uijg=)[[77]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAJHzi3d9QsYRWZsigYLpl25OJEEMgADDcU_b7D6qTbVTcQ8qx9kvY2j4ISmFM1dsX5E0N2XlEeFcsj9N-R8VgGvv74VOnPqt11_CwPiM_VPle2oNJR0JaxymkpAgh2KvBMijFlwTeHAB3oCPFnpf0BuNd_xp3-ZQBd5XcHHFFf7E9tbS-0=).
*   **Forecasting Models:** Utilize statistical methods to predict future financial performance.
*   **Option Pricing Models:** Calculate the fair value of options (e.g., binomial model).
*   **Sensitivity Analysis Model:** Tests how changes in input variables affect model output [[76]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXENf8Iub5t5tqoEafW3AJDFo0FTyvsYl2VeSjD_6-4M357TgV4a6dArt78ijeGabgqSSROuzR1d8o7_Wl5C_kvPh6M0eiHUPoOkVZkvbO07M4AENEofPFoZJJULOPFUGHHGf973fc8Y3qrOkXQzkv9qGq9ItzvmTL4=).
*   **Stress Testing Models:** Quantify potential losses under adverse conditions.
*   **Credit Risk Models:** Quantify potential losses from credit defaults [[78]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAKDVA2G2zcGsY5kRWj2WU0-Sa7HUSCKpTfE0TggJsL8-_fGXRQZ5eFhm4lPbO9fz-lSmli3zFW7BG1pu9rjtSsK04cK9f4jvcNqHl9UbR_2RaE9L-tMdcdrRySw-UTIp5rat3_o04nP3Jq7SZf4r2ptT06ipueyPyHE6hPQG7QuGNwGHg==).
*   **Present Value Formula Model:** Used to evaluate expected returns.
*   **Linear Programming Model:** Used for optimization problems.
*   **Risk Utility Function Model:** Models investor risk preferences [[77]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAJHzi3d9QsYRWZsigYLpl25OJEEMgADDcU_b7D6qTbVTcQ8qx9kvY2j4ISmFM1dsX5E0N2XlEeFcsj9N-R8VgGvv74VOnPqt11_CwPiM_VPle2oNJR0JaxymkpAgh2KvBMijFlwTeHAB3oCPFnpf0BuNd_xp3-ZQBd5XcHHFFf7E9tbS-0=).
*   **Optimization Models:** Find the best solution given constraints.
*   **Simulation Models:** Create scenarios to understand potential outcomes [[78]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAKDVA2G2zcGsY5kRWj2WU0-Sa7HUSCKpTfE0TggJsL8-_fGXRQZ5eFhm4lPbO9fz-lSmli3zFW7BG1pu9rjtSsK04cK9f4jvcNqHl9UbR_2RaE9L-tMdcdrRySw-UTIp5rat3_o04nP3Jq7SZf4r2ptT06ipueyPyHE6hPQG7QuGNwGHg==).

### **Physical Science Thinking Models**

Principles from physics and engineering provide frameworks for understanding systems, risk, and competitive forces [[3]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXGv0w970LpzkK9UUMMTmq9v0Fs5J1xcDJOsLrYwwwSTXBmxT-Zlar0oZzFtQSLmRLTFBcTuCU_Tk5BOcfCGnDAQPSRRfE7w4R_G013bwAxNwywlgX-7PaccxJKe8s-dpzBxaVhQF-ruW6gchNe0QTHghI0Dk08QYH5elfk-vg==)[[60]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAIX62hcCZOeJjn3tb0HYJR-azF_YKqKv_I72Rt8H4be3yc-sdTuf4z_Q7WBWdqVKinHDtpm4m1fNddiugueBNp_qtVOpiev6enQj4iaUgcfhBMbr_2bDX6PrxUh6hxQeZ4VDwsyk_FwCdeZUqzcNoE-_KP2hthNdy30Wlnga3IZ-op8OpDVzJVKpSnhiTFM88mPZMGfvaLeavXi3g==)[[57]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAJEqWlIx_K-A5yclorW4lcPOyvZNErVSNqSIpjJgBfPiVZoMhg67-oMkvLjYgGeSNP53Ns5gBSXnDvrr7FBtkyOq9i7TTcZkjpvZmtdDeWDqzbEa20IqRlPNMX9B3MVnr7pr_1qrTCLX8JUAYhsbl--MeeDhHyMZB7_EDiqzwtSdJuBAPoB5gJU8OyrAESZ1RM4X_2qspnAleYuFFYfXoV7WX490GwDBtlIWeQwoJjSYN6MRiQ5G_B9_xTKe2Ea0pRY_llaEA==)[[62]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqALXGJVPRY5RAzcHOCzc98JLQz3e20mckl1PETKaZ4YgNkm4zC1gYNqpRacj3pzuCv9CUYKe9UkLnjtk45CplPApraTBGgdQT5wZzzYf3doGdtvaGfh0_wgVB8J8ULPd5g_HezZqL6QiYZ62m4plLR2P2N5ZEZGvSUD7e7joWY4AxkeLmQ4TfOhYggwMNjw1Yz29EA6z_jAq1lmZ88NdtFd-WYrxZz4jBu5TdRMh)[[31]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAKorpJiCPcKnKTPUmfgXDmPLUYziVhVNmP8556YCzz1mCH59klRCRo0o3oyuzDhktT2roF6piBehBLVkvlLdYRkU5U0CbN2CdSO6n3aou4IhHks88TsgVjh5uBFxGGYD8WZut87LByGdZhjVMSwCNfBAaU8CFg2uFMn9il_dQnd59Or93QPyVyo)[[32]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAL2MDT234jOPDrCEIrRJDTSPJtJ_mO3Ex_lLLhWrHBZNwAlukUOqeC-dZ3wRhFQ0SRWvSWgMucqU7xE7Ka63OymYrr9PBPmlgTvay4-PY1ptSKjRbmEhRoBM9ib4xbshqivxxvvFfyROXRpj4m-3kEVkl_3_RzU4Dk0Tog8SUTTzhY001ud_CKOFRDFm-VWuIql)[[46]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAJq5ItGosa1nwXIxPhFx8VA7tniB6m4pRtLcfwffvno533g5jbMQ1GzMewUoepJCUCn9phQJwDTWQtFUacj66ROvBs1ekHArkYEvultwuebxTu1VeZs1KwRCcYRx5snTpF5Nokc5diyY3iCr_9optNidViJYC5P30Ys1yrgZxtvj5W2sMmqKFgu4OWEh362h8wkBNNKOSh3z96iwUe3R **Examples of Relevant Physical Science Principles:**

*   **Margin of Safety:** Analogous to engineering design where structures are built to withstand loads far beyond expectations [[60]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAIX62hcCZOeJjn3tb0HYJR-azF_YKqKv_I72Rt8H4be3yc-sdTuf4z_Q7WBWdqVKinHDtpm4m1fNddiugueBNp_qtVOpiev6enQj4iaUgcfhBMbr_2bDX6PrxUh6hxQeZ4VDwsyk_FwCdeZUqzcNoE-_KP2hthNdy30Wlnga3IZ-op8OpDVzJVKpSnhiTFM88mPZMGfvaLeavXi3g==)[[61]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAI5uoYkWJTU9W_KO-XVQdQG3G_57XxFAO_Q-9siGBD63DKf2deHOTlvRdlB_BFNjrq-JB5mE-lrDR2lL6TZo6RZKARiq2Tan7m7XvkraEfbImf-8ZQlCk4CdQVUS_MncvsI5E6TfZxIbKWidrEWcqmGrfeB_aN0QiKnHQGYmXsNLGYdlUgPeIixTXBA3N885bwMAD4yiKkiWVcebA==).
*   **Circle of Competence:** Similar to building expertise in a scientific field through focused study [[57]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAJEqWlIx_K-A5yclorW4lcPOyvZNErVSNqSIpjJgBfPiVZoMhg67-oMkvLjYgGeSNP53Ns5gBSXnDvrr7FBtkyOq9i7TTcZkjpvZmtdDeWDqzbEa20IqRlPNMX9B3MVnr7pr_1qrTCLX8JUAYhsbl--MeeDhHyMZB7_EDiqzwtSdJuBAPoB5gJU8OyrAESZ1RM4X_2qspnAleYuFFYfXoV7WX490GwDBtlIWeQwoJjSYN6MRiQ5G_B9_xTKe2Ea0pRY_llaEA==)[[46]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAJq5ItGosa1nwXIxPhFx8VA7tniB6m4pRtLcfwffvno533g5jbMQ1GzMewUoepJCUCn9phQJwDTWQtFUacj66ROvBs1ekHArkYEvultwuebxTu1VeZs1KwRCcYRx5snTpF5Nokc5diyY3iCr_9optNidViJYC5P30Ys1yrgZxtvj5W2sMmqKFgu4OWEh362h8wkBNNKOSh3z96iwUe3R5no9KMKrAShH9PWcoppLF2FgJKG5gRwnmsyKr9Q6NDmAkI80dctpg==).
*   **Economic "Moats":** Like ecological systems where certain species have advantages [[62]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqALXGJVPRY5RAzcHOCzc98JLQz3e20mckl1PETKaZ4YgNkm4zC1gYNqpRacj3pzuCv9CUYKe9UkLnjtk45CplPApraTBGgdQT5wZzzYf3doGdtvaGfh0_wgVB8J8ULPd5g_HezZqL6QiYZ62m4plLR2P2N5ZEZGvSUD7e7joWY4AxkeLmQ4TfOhYggwMNjw1Yz29EA6z_jAq1lmZ88NdtFd-WYrxZz4jBu5TdRMh)[[46]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAJq5ItGosa1nwXIxPhFx8VA7tniB6m4pRtLcfwffvno533g5jbMQ1GzMewUoepJCUCn9phQJwDTWQtFUacj66ROvBs1ekHArkYEvultwuebxTu1VeZs1KwRCcYRx5snTpF5Nokc5diyY3iCr_9optNidViJYC5P30Ys1yrgZxtvj5W2sMmqKFgu4OWEh362h8wkBNNKOSh3z96iwUe3R5no9KMKrAShH9PWcoppLF2FgJKG5gRwnmsyKr9Q6NDmAkI80dctpg==)[[33]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAI5MX0oQE-Hy3jR6DwBXObPU3zSU4YE5S7HKdXk7GCbJuE2HhuV0tyg65Xptu2pg7EppyYrNkwQWVs8IFbhZEXA8oolcm_ua6pgCGtwwCiNvmhaNlVQKnvxjRnMGi3X24oYHn7nrI1S4PnMkyfSfMtnfJKXcgLFeDcTUTmwu5L4-6Zy46at8Aj_iMwpBlc10G3BFnfzdnD8w4SfdNFfO6kb9yqMPwGfkAex4CkaIB22NfDof5eTrbTBFbxYFw==).
*   **Inversion:** A common problem-solving technique in science where problems are looked at backwards [[62]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqALXGJVPRY5RAzcHOCzc98JLQz3e20mckl1PETKaZ4YgNkm4zC1gYNqpRacj3pzuCv9CUYKe9UkLnjtk45CplPApraTBGgdQT5wZzzYf3doGdtvaGfh0_wgVB8J8ULPd5g_HezZqL6QiYZ62m4plLR2P2N5ZEZGvSUD7e7joWY4AxkeLmQ4TfOhYggwMNjw1Yz29EA6z_jAq1lmZ88NdtFd-WYrxZz4jBu5TdRMh).
*   **Compounding:** Exponential growth, like radioactive decay or population growth [[57]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAJEqWlIx_K-A5yclorW4lcPOyvZNErVSNqSIpjJgBfPiVZoMhg67-oMkvLjYgGeSNP53Ns5gBSXnDvrr7FBtkyOq9i7TTcZkjpvZmtdDeWDqzbEa20IqRlPNMX9B3MVnr7pr_1qrTCLX8JUAYhsbl--MeeDhHyMZB7_EDiqzwtSdJuBAPoB5gJU8OyrAESZ1RM4X_2qspnAleYuFFYfXoV7WX490GwDBtlIWeQwoJjSYN6MRiQ5G_B9_xTKe2Ea0pRY_llaEA==)[[31]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAKorpJiCPcKnKTPUmfgXDmPLUYziVhVNmP8556YCzz1mCH59klRCRo0o3oyuzDhktT2roF6piBehBLVkvlLdYRkU5U0CbN2CdSO6n3aou4IhHks88TsgVjh5uBFxGGYD8WZut87LByGdZhjVMSwCNfBAaU8CFg2uFMn9il_dQnd59Or93QPyVyo).
*   **Critical Mass:** In nuclear physics, the minimum amount needed for a chain reaction [[79]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXHLKbcr91i3cpCCoL66zjnUN0iD425Rg0wGdLPXT21UH7GCdTS7btWAw963pppdwKIvUp8LLru7Sqh4s9ZAzPpyJPv7kEMwdCdDU5fFAqoE3stkPWqHQhXF8XSl0DT53vcr29idEgI=)[[80]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXGF1X_B8UfXxWbFajZR5cYeMRtlkJhbaxi3PTtnIJkZwgLRG5jsM9EqNdyUvHAQ7OsJdk0nN9EySQ1TF-WXfzWIhMiyEGt2lp2RuCzyedPMw5CNXA8jkX_lDEF8pPpuCfx_xYFnM7b49AwLPg==)[[81]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXGF8FiTNtl8_ITTK6zbHXbD_APN5Gp1MefBMHdM-2uLPg6lbPBAiEsfVg2xIBvRZgidHSx4m1kMbztWTWROre7blh6vHPZDsayNWWX9uK3-Vu_dbXXI2EncpL8SNVhINR9KizhBzrqM0W_ZNXtu7xlVkMiFG-V-AtI3Z-P-xb8xAniIZonX-Mf6Xpb64UyvbBecL9z74m6rhVzJhg==)[[82]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXGUE-9g5mhulrulYL6Su9xiFidUID71_vZT5IYe-796WXbLp-UGPcB0Kt77PzEiNMS2HrQbosO3coPdRfXs4QWly-RM3kDLc_oiZLAlymZ1eRgHk6zDsMI98SFWFNXwB7fVKsc3KDi0a2CoogG-fiKqoDnpiQWhE9B2VJWQofzQhHyJsHrNHliBIMI3jnXyYuSt4CBzVd_dMNkTdF3NXedGox01ZaqBxnX4BMPNFMxsW8pOhSfTmGBmXmRlX_d4DvPI-YY3PSqF6xRXrOrROyyIpv1UvWYZUWfXMnLmCsov8XBmwlWg6MdAnZpc8okajkuQ7zufKl7Eqs3rLtAMAMnM5ik_geGQWlXar2PEqZQWl_M=). In business, the minimum amount of users, customers, funding, etc., needed for self-sustaining growth [[83]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXFMWQ3GJ8-noIPJYiF5AVQqytz6BxlsTYgnGCd1Bus7HOr3E4tzT59ObEtWG9wkSHKabgdy5bJYeVxUBSc7r598-RdwVnN6O435j4U_eOqCxfSmSQ7-Gxy1K_XWDjIr2N6FPZubTKyHmUVN-_c6AtXQ).
*   **Leverage:** Understanding how small inputs can create large outputs.
*   **Inertia:** Resistance to change, applicable to market trends or organizational behavior [[3]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXGv0w970LpzkK9UUMMTmq9v0Fs5J1xcDJOsLrYwwwSTXBmxT-Zlar0oZzFtQSLmRLTFBcTuCU_Tk5BOcfCGnDAQPSRRfE7w4R_G013bwAxNwywlgX-7PaccxJKe8s-dpzBxaVhQF-ruW6gchNe0QTHghI0Dk08QYH5elfk-vg==).
*   **Simplicity:** Seeking understandable systems, like simple machines [[33]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAI5MX0oQE-Hy3jR6DwBXObPU3zSU4YE5S7HKdXk7GCbJuE2HhuV0tyg65Xptu2pg7EppyYrNkwQWVs8IFbhZEXA8oolcm_ua6pgCGtwwCiNvmhaNlVQKnvxjRnMGi3X24oYHn7nrI1S4PnMkyfSfMtnfJKXcgLFeDcTUTmwu5L4-6Zy46at8Aj_iMwpBlc10G3BFnfzdnD8w4SfdNFfO6kb9yqMPwGfkAex4CkaIB22NfDof5eTrbTBFbxYFw==).

### **Biological Thinking Models**

Biology offers insights into adaptation, ecosystems, and complex systems [[3]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXGv0w970LpzkK9UUMMTmq9v0Fs5J1xcDJOsLrYwwwSTXBmxT-Zlar0oZzFtQSLmRLTFBcTuCU_Tk5BOcfCGnDAQPSRRfE7w4R_G013bwAxNwywlgX-7PaccxJKe8s-dpzBxaVhQF-ruW6gchNe0QTHghI0Dk08QYH5elfk-vg==)[[84]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAIjZbNf60Pvlp5zfgzVNQUXr--phYtcEzv3KymxhdEthe-3FOjlHkwVyLHyoDK0eVFSaJP4DSde4LIUxMNXA7b6g2diZLHsIkaw-tZqaPBQo5MjoKLWyy-q0Vn-RyJhanM3dhML1cIO-qhjMZAM4PaR29mIKccTr9o_xMpdwPIPdDzaE8q26vZrCbplEzGQ3CkazntFUuUvcKvLL7H4Zzszwg==)[[85]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAIjd1D0Txo-IB_YYHhguhrJK50iBxagRxttmFgT0aaet02AgZ2aA4bo893duc1OpQgsDJI75X-CN52YoY_c8muRhrCmh8H16mmU9e5SMUvE_rtppBkh_TUagR9ID7drqJ7TclfmTWxO5-pOvxYCUkwi1e5jfTJ5iPlGZ_l9324QwPMwp-f2k1uumVQM1_WBo-wHmlqXwLa3tx_5GcdqdQ==)[[86]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqALbKQYTojxR058FllFto-UaUvIYYrcbAYZjeaGyi3odd1Yd6ue3OLEIxg4RrQcvux9bYq7-uwlOgIMjicq1ULhIIb-DhxXvIaFbIvnv4lSwShIbpWmc2DRB4oHX19rwzvJRcE2k8hHY1fmI3q-acBww1sfmhPcR84A=)[[87]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAK3eqFD7DFknwv5ENQhfXLXb2sWKFDf3x4sL5Rc89Ln8hpn4lOLstJam8izfGRrKt-Uy6YG6DghQmoCEXfdyXdm6T15V5iO3E9iaswbOVA-rPPw94T2qR1vqHY-Dfe3ovFilI0LyMuVCFVwO17RzuHVFsdowtY02nfmJZUQNW86OEgBGaeoSCunJcxkv-9QwQ==).

**Examples of Relevant Biological Models:**

*   **Model Organisms:** Studying exemplar companies like Google or Toyota to understand business models, similar to biologists studying fruit flies [[84]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAIjZbNf60Pvlp5zfgzVNQUXr--phYtcEzv3KymxhdEthe-3FOjlHkwVyLHyoDK0eVFSaJP4DSde4LIUxMNXA7b6g2diZLHsIkaw-tZqaPBQo5MjoKLWyy-q0Vn-RyJhanM3dhML1cIO-qhjMZAM4PaR29mIKccTr9o_xMpdwPIPdDzaE8q26vZrCbplEzGQ3CkazntFUuUvcKvLL7H4Zzszwg==).
*   **Ecosystems:** Viewing businesses as interconnected parts of larger systems.
*   **Complex Adaptive Systems:** Understanding that local interactions can lead to unpredictable global effects [[85]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAIjd1D0Txo-IB_YYHhguhrJK50iBxagRxttmFgT0aaet02AgZ2aA4bo893duc1OpQgsDJI75X-CN52YoY_c8muRhrCmh8H16mmU9e5SMUvE_rtppBkh_TUagR9ID7drqJ7TclfmTWxO5-pOvxYCUkwi1e5jfTJ5iPlGZ_l9324QwPMwp-f2k1uumVQM1_WBo-wHmlqXwLa3tx_5GcdqdQ==).
*   **Evolution:** Businesses need to adapt and innovate to survive, avoiding the "success trap".
*   **Risk Management:** Biological systems have backup mechanisms; businesses need to foresee and manage system-wide risks [[85]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAIjd1D0Txo-IB_YYHhguhrJK50iBxagRxttmFgT0aaet02AgZ2aA4bo893duc1OpQgsDJI75X-CN52YoY_c8muRhrCmh8H16mmU9e5SMUvE_rtppBkh_TUagR9ID7drqJ7TclfmTWxO5-pOvxYCUkwi1e5jfTJ5iPlGZ_l9324QwPMwp-f2k1uumVQM1_WBo-wHmlqXwLa3tx_5GcdqdQ==)[[86]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqALbKQYTojxR058FllFto-UaUvIYYrcbAYZjeaGyi3odd1Yd6ue3OLEIxg4RrQcvux9bYq7-uwlOgIMjicq1ULhIIb-DhxXvIaFbIvnv4lSwShIbpWmc2DRB4oHX19rwzvJRcE2k8hHY1fmI3q-acBww1sfmhPcR84A=).
*   **Collaboration and Purpose:** Successful biological systems rely on collaboration; businesses can foster trust by defining a clear purpose [[85]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAIjd1D0Txo-IB_YYHhguhrJK50iBxagRxttmFgT0aaet02AgZ2aA4bo893duc1OpQgsDJI75X-CN52YoY_c8muRhrCmh8H16mmU9e5SMUvE_rtppBkh_TUagR9ID7drqJ7TclfmTWxO5-pOvxYCUkwi1e5jfTJ5iPlGZ_l9324QwPMwp-f2k1uumVQM1_WBo-wHmlqXwLa3tx_5GcdqdQ==).
*   **Biological Modeling:** Logistic growth models can be used to predict market trends [[87]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAK3eqFD7DFknwv5ENQhfXLXb2sWKFDf3x4sL5Rc89Ln8hpn4lOLstJam8izfGRrKt-Uy6YG6DghQmoCEXfdyXdm6T15V5iO3E9iaswbOVA-rPPw94T2qR1vqHY-Dfe3ovFilI0LyMuVCFVwO17RzuHVFsdowtY02nfmJZUQNW86OEgBGaeoSCunJcxkv-9QwQ==).

### **Economic Thinking Models**

Economics provides frameworks for understanding markets, incentives, and value creation *   **Network Effects:** Value increases as more people use a product or service [[83]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXFMWQ3GJ8-noIPJYiF5AVQqytz6BxlsTYgnGCd1Bus7HOr3E4tzT59ObEtWG9wkSHKabgdy5bJYeVxUBSc7r598-RdwVnN6O435j4U_eOqCxfSmSQ7-Gxy1K_XWDjIr2N6FPZubTKyHmUVN-_c6AtXQ)[[62]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqALXGJVPRY5RAzcHOCzc98JLQz3e20mckl1PETKaZ4YgNkm4zC1gYNqpRacj3pzuCv9CUYKe9UkLnjtk45CplPApraTBGgdQT5wZzzYf3doGdtvaGfh0_wgVB8J8ULPd5g_HezZqL6QiYZ62m4plLR2P2N5ZEZGvSUD7e7joWY4AxkeLmQ4TfOhYggwMNjw1Yz29EA6z_jAq1lmZ88NdtFd-WYrxZz4jBu5TdRMh)[[46]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAJq5ItGosa1nwXIxPhFx8VA7tniB6m4pRtLcfwffvno533g5jbMQ1GzMewUoepJCUCn9phQJwDTWQtFUacj66ROvBs1ekHArkYEvultwuebxTu1VeZs1KwRCcYRx5snTpF5Nokc5diyY3iCr_9optNidViJYC5P30Ys1yrgZxtvj5W2sMmqKFgu4OWEh362h8wkBNNKOSh3z96iwUe3R5no9KMKrAShH9PWcoppLF2FgJKG5gRwnmsyKr9Q6NDmAkI80dctpg==)[[66]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqALByU1pMCr_V_GfLpnUkUuQbJ7lTcPgh5BnJKa8xYyUiQCImZCEB9Y9d7tV2WRf5jVpPdqkgjVdGp97zUnMglmKs_JoT288DId49Zw2qXWrBwfXAE0p2sAheCYyiZBMVFB8pbaywxY9EPkWzU4duWbEhci04RykJn94aFv_Iyz2-4_TvL9W_nWCGAcR1HFapOelkhwhLgPUjOl73Co9mj0koZ1j9D6O735oPUcF).
*   **Competitive Advantage ("Economic Moats"):** Durable features that protect a business from rivals (e.g., strong brands, patents, regulations) [[16]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXF-ltZz9QW5DaMLuoPQUTM4jjEyylFb0PV0qeZq27kixsjRVl_7Isgc4hufjPKnkYtFIdoSBtnexbEVhqnahmC1oXYutVI1r4Q0Rzx_MlwXy3j024E1vOmhskUt5vWAhP1Rkn5ZJKh2RTVEj1BpXD1KIPyGpm_b93dktYL3bFIfmmCh8qPpyS3pbNd4iVXcFGc=)[[17]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXGMgMeXCWntpSKBaNMklmbCwYEim9e7zI95mKgFLSa52zi0BRpiXSPmCEaAyym7ZX-oVqPb6MFA7FNrgqPRlm44Ys-DfNPe86sNRrZvZOrH18QHGyfLJBSm1azToSW60vRo_m8l-hbcgSbKQVvKh2FOe6-gBbj_kMXsWptzXpi-J-SVABhLSUGsxq-Nhup17XIlH8kaT5xW)[[4]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXHcSTGOAV6ceJ9x7bwI8btxAf0izZGwviSoNqQm5GwdFyQvHbFzL6KPCH9PcXKKS4LsgyaJgJxOJ9FW7QvUJwItcsetBERbgDJ3BSZ_3YLUOaGCxj3RrQt8owe1-A2YXdbbrJY48RwWLMb5xiwivq87pPxrnyIHW2tRLQWCbpBgsPhaWg==)[[12]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXHZITiztt-MyYTU3qm3rwjAr1eHCrEwBkycdDMJJWBGdx4UDzhUdYYmpzjZsZ9zLgIndRRvcOTKtrHDVqkwMZ_V1Be3KmjHIk3TpK8lMbz77E9bHUut2Tcqp0FCyBe5-t6pakzBwFc-bQ6QtlyZzXW4lm3DGmiXPlKposy2dEhxMGofk_eAcbLQV5gPOqJk2S2iMvvES9hB)[[43]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXESM3Nc5_coO_H1l4r7VkVqHUknMQMniOi_ORUTJqMtdc3cnDb_j3R-A9tw80Q0fVGWKiwu_vCrAFwxOMg8UcXuEpNeSUj039iMg8Z82O_sdT6OX0qkoVi0XBkhp5aZFJOgCvdGGLJvXfQCrZKaisCjc4Pnn620zwhnQzmbMTP_qhYthFchZrOQVtU1TNSWWMY=)[[57]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAJEqWlIx_K-A5yclorW4lcPOyvZNErVSNqSIpjJgBfPiVZoMhg67-oMkvLjYgGeSNP53Ns5gBSXnDvrr7FBtkyOq9i7TTcZkjpvZmtdDeWDqzbEa20IqRlPNMX9B3MVnr7pr_1qrTCLX8JUAYhsbl--MeeDhHyMZB7_EDiqzwtSdJuBAPoB5gJU8OyrAESZ1RM4X_2qspnAleYuFFYfXoV7WX490GwDBtlIWeQwoJjSYN6MRiQ5G_B9_xTKe2Ea0pRY_llaEA==)[[62]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqALXGJVPRY5RAzcHOCzc98JLQz3e20mckl1PETKaZ4YgNkm4zC1gYNqpRacj3pzuCv9CUYKe9UkLnjtk45CplPApraTBGgdQT5wZzzYf3doGdtvaGfh0_wgVB8J8ULPd5g_HezZqL6QiYZ62m4plLR2P2N5ZEZGvSUD7e7joWY4AxkeLmQ4TfOhYggwMNjw1Yz29EA6z_jAq1lmZ88NdtFd-WYrxZz4jBu5Td *   **Intrinsic Value:** The true worth of a business, independent of market price [[12]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXHZITiztt-MyYTU3qm3rwjAr1eHCrEwBkycdDMJJWBGdx4UDzhUdYYmpzjZsZ9zLgIndRRvcOTKtrHDVqkwMZ_V1Be3KmjHIk3TpK8lMbz77E9bHUut2Tcqp0FCyBe5-t6pakzBwFc-bQ6QtlyZzXW4lm3DGmiXPlKposy2dEhxMGofk_eAcbLQV5gPOqJk2S2iMvvES9hB)[[13]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXEjYQFogGVnsdwF0-iJTlQO73eDyGoLQiLi5pvw8YB-xAE2DlBmrlrf6YovitiyQOVAviGXyKEYVp5L77lVuayp2iGRtebAp6GaFFHYxzm_oqER0Iv0tb4RWYeQDx9EIJROkceoj5fkvfUuEw4AH9h-3QKgwBaCxSYJ4RNL7O_N8uudNU6_1KIcImzS5N6WH-T5178BGgU=)[[14]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAL4s9uHOwBA1TO4futw03DoWyp8cuwGsaf59ow_SN07euz5yHYyW_DNFxG7474-ZjNKwHA9AKD9hGAWGGmslmUDawuaUKalAoqMGfgkYbtqKorPeK_t8f0c4fYH6Bh5MTMg83gYQT7UZiwZ-gRveTMccPIXP0XXKyiphkKGplXQKOVAJk6ITG6heWWjcrfdOuS13uR1yjAKiA==).

### **Application of Multidisciplinary Thinking**

Munger applied his multidisciplinary approach to all aspects of decision-making, particularly in investment [[3]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXGv0w970LpzkK9UUMMTmq9v0Fs5J1xcDJOsLrYwwwSTXBmxT-Zlar0oZzFtQSLmRLTFBcTuCU_Tk5BOcfCGnDAQPSRRfE7w4R_G013bwAxNwywlgX-7PaccxJKe8s-dpzBxaVhQF-ruW6gchNe0QTHghI0Dk08QYH5elfk-vg==)[[4]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXHcSTGOAV6ceJ9x7bwI8btxAf0izZGwviSoNqQm5GwdFyQvHbFzL6KPCH9PcXKKS4LsgyaJgJxOJ9FW7QvUJwItcsetBERbgDJ3BSZ_3YLUOaGCxj3RrQt8owe1-A2YXdbbrJY48RwWLMb5xiwivq87pPxrnyIHW2tRLQWCbpBgsPhaWg==)[[5]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAI5LGeNaQDpXPqGbKUF9A6W5iM7iDEGe7GJ72kUqNNdMnkBfsKho0dnIKDAhpXoA3NpXxxAGz9Y9l2LmREntV4orSConlPoMoRJUSKpZlRdX7pRYRWw8tH4LIUT475uIOux)[[6]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAL-BRklsGE62uLUxkzFV_uDCiIIEqFW0ddrETUxhNU-OFUE0rO6FFZFnvTqdhBFCkPRMO-P2hHdOHfS6StgNcArRu57cqGQaTHp2Tb1nVDIoBHmy9iUtbiLom1Crp-NYtNxGebslgqLNOVt2jEIO4kZsL9WPltFx3WekZP913UcSWMJrpfabB6UmfJJRv-cypD8U91c8e-tPdRVbzyQoXOeZKeaKXTRDwMm)[[38]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqALGtD3vTRxpL0lUM3SLyIyZehx3ivYu8A2U1kCqD8zmzT--Z_02mnspQ-Ub2B24Hzd0_fJZhqWaI8U6GdRESdT4t-z9Bl8eUO33WhencTU9ihtXjLi4Z5jjIUgq-IyeWEthYVdTF0k=)[[39]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAIStEqI4zqTHOgo47nGPsnxBEJ5SuNf9BAnt7OODdqY6TEFJF3Kq5BQ8rP3BNgeRMD-GU8Ke996j6eWWo_JykO7EuKoKdNVWUh4gVML-XaBXGsfUNXXLLrwzHWb2R-Meny5uP6HNg-tTwBqEW05m6b28vLHxk7rn80Pe2p2x1-uYlmWvFt1rECbaG_kfEHGAdXFFfoguWeSSNwgOAYqx1chdkuNTmfNyk8T)[[40]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAJq00KFaR2Sg3fQhopUOBAOgC_h7nyCfvKVQAStbHloIVn2GM1Fdx28OJmO23vK57lV_H4KLLIkqc5Z82WmT4gHndljffLTywmwANWvqB2_Q59L1U7MbOEr0pxo92WCwDKWciVDcuM=)[[41]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAJuLqwcOUC48mJKpQPaR4tUjdvLVVA9RS_2m57nq4v3vmMYH8sEWMExwSHjXnYOwomd-su2fNcWc2OP4Iq0pE3uhWf8dYqraOXF2k7sdIeX7aj_N88ZlcA_E-PI940LI0Mlxo1I7FARGn2MZJ64L6zww07numzAOKwpn-0R4kN9NaJ2lsvHzlgxv *   **Ethical Businesses:** He preferred companies with fair, even-handed, and ethical models [[16]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXF-ltZz9QW5DaMLuoPQUTM4jjEyylFb0PV0qeZq27kixsjRVl_7Isgc4hufjPKnkYtFIdoSBtnexbEVhqnahmC1oXYutVI1r4Q0Rzx_MlwXy3j024E1vOmhskUt5vWAhP1Rkn5ZJKh2RTVEj1BpXD1KIPyGpm_b93dktYL3bFIfmmCh8qPpyS3pbNd4iVXcFGc=)[[43]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AbF9wXESM3Nc5_coO_H1l4r7VkVqHUknMQMniOi_ORUTJqMtdc3cnDb_j3R-A9tw80Q0fVGWKiwu_vCrAFwxOMg8UcXuEpNeSUj039iMg8Z82O_sdT6OX0qkoVi0XBkhp5aZFJOgCvdGGLJvXfQCrZKaisCjc4Pnn620zwhnQzmbMTP_qhYthFchZrOQVtU1TNSWWMY=)[[32]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAL2MDT234jOPDrCEIrRJDTSPJtJ_mO3Ex_lLLhWrHBZNwAlukUOqeC-dZ3wRhFQ0SRWvSWgMucqU7xE7Ka63OymYrr9PBPmlgTvay4-PY1ptSKjRbmEhRoBM9ib4xbshqivxxvvFfyROXRpj4m-3kEVkl_3_RzU4Dk0Tog8SUTTzhY001ud_CKOFRDFm-VWuIql)[[21]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAJcZtdyc1dKggjpQgtEAMo07KKlrHCwVcaTFc1rF2ScMNk2pegJSQctekktODRHvix-yVvfCKvVdpgOaV-m3XqxBkC73WUFwVbRUf40ie-rioM12BPl49TlF9OkB9ly5VncL5j-ReqSrh8l6KqmhocvZQKOWjShjQthZ6luvdo-6_g4eGPsou5kWQh0Ij4tLn_qfNd4QXQ4Ury2bVRU)[[88]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAKvVBhvHnfqfvcEBnnb-Wi6k33CaLOtmuqHeR-UplVoKDqs_Q38LxEKCCRcMBBmPezQ0sPGACkdZ8aW6PeVbrid4lcz3JV7gbV_5zVP8nH1HGYf93A5grw4cOgkGcBURgJf2EopnqQc89dpgyqm3YT8vVcRu2OcZ4pXlU4RuMhyKmQjsoiFM8j44AtMM8Dp0M3G)[[55]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAIxIC9dk6CeB6XxE4nyugF9CXhkPc3EbtemGzc1WO8AkLCov8ATz229sQ7TwsBoi3iKSE9dZHVojNZgVIFjOZb_E3xi2FAcki3G8CqXzdYXtr3Ar7vMF60vT7plOrj1Psnam7ZySUTmKLdCCOO3q5xmNFwrx8yoT0C0VKWft99EFKQXfi-ReA0L9ednM8467QlTYtgeRuBK87zRZobf77X-lr70QfBzExzWUILIiBZ7cGqlThEJ_xIJQPdatRfIriEDfkBB-SLlPOQlNwoLivAi)[[34]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAImwMKQJ4KvxtlNuysrHlgrfs29NN8K2v9p2IPYRRpJlJo3hA2aFdw8ER9yGyhaKU9obsvpClEIgb8LS26utm_bL3wQRDEyh8N7q4ACov5ZTODujX0niZVMWJgPsTjaL45pWDAASwXe9dRga3eot8lAlOB9OzOjjlIb18hsi3rFBIIr-TdrDndUKnZc9FWBqysH)[[2 *   **Examples of Investments:**
    *   **Burlington Northern Santa Fe (BNSF):** Railroads have high barriers to entry (moat).
    *   **Berkshire Hathaway Energy (BHE):** Utilities have high capital requirements (moat).
    *   **Insurance Float:** A unique competitive advantage for Berkshire.
    *   **Apple, Inc:** Strong brand and customer loyalty (moat) [[65]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAIxgswiY6c9x73toBvBhqEh2UjWAP6ti6S2NjkBRne8qNCe98VgDjWFgylHSJQ5VWTANM3-PiWZmR4YF2qYQn9R3JM43RFq2lW0ISNfA3sUcPP0ekbzlA6uy1KqrLsoXFPlk5TTYGwHKzTwSU4rUNuPPac=).
    *   **Wal-Mart:** Economies of scale in distribution (moat).
    *   **See's Candies, Geico:** Examples of businesses with moats in the Berkshire portfolio [[64]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAJKyck9t7IuMWbLhUviNFYuu7uT_DY-EvBqXfXKMqYpvRPcgBOmuitRIY8XItm4KoX0cal5NzHpTvB_d371vc7reBKWeYLChs8rP378FGNrHKeexSrvKI1cYzmbjZ7mt-PaYeMVaIPEqzRQUB3KmuFwflNX_cydpsytvnQoFO7Ssft3yCfiR29PPU8S5fgaL_PzK6g=).
    *   **Financial Sector:** Investments in Wells Fargo, Bank of America, U.S. Bancorp.
    *   **POSCO Holdings Inc:** International materials company.
    *   **Alibaba Group Holding Ltd:** An investment later considered a mistake [[1]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAKLjvICgvzYMPxvt_Mj8cW9bN4cX6NgpCLb9xPMLygZUctIUZgFj0NG6-OQeXeV4MCZsVyhRIX7xsdHnUp2vIMdYZ_sLjo0r7lP0RWaINZqlNCG9dZoxkyjCUhiJiL8YykOVRsip9CryuFPcg==).
    *   **Costco Wholesale:** Munger served on the board [[2]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAJgYmTmoqqo1XAMoxkiIvk-YbKHS4L9AwiEYR5c8ZnE7A7XIE6uLxFxuoia1zfFBCl0_lsF5NB_UrCON0jImbWJbjSypLiYphsk1nMFeI6GSqxEHIQpyN7o5uru_5fF2KJbXAe1N8v3vmltFDYDxIppr6K-NAHaOZk23lH_u7dUkq6rcdwTuCGY).

### **Influences on Munger's Thinking**

Munger's philosophy was shaped by various experiences and figures [[8]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAKx-ZCkraECpw2zpP3qVl6zL_kCwoSRIIQms84mnJ3E49BeG-kOeopfxzDFZ40PiUAEn1cR5ZqNJ9j0Sby6BQSF68aP5at43eEUVsycOsxUjuZjKY0qNb0jonsJRHBaOY5t9QZqnZLEZ7YtQ1VrvJs55mRIbyoN4c_Ki4gsNpBGfKt8z43S)[[9]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAKXLueM8ZuT3A8vgRpHvN-PQexxg3Z1hpcB2BeeVLkmF5l6VWceGZ7cLE1xJ7fXMJ2S4YYYgcQUsJHPt4bKnbNmbOQuykdO62WHXejx96OuSLkxmb-TmiOjvf_Fjq5gF2YjRCOGBgTfxt79Tg-NSqtdvxjKYiVCixTdwmSzhALvj180UA==)[[89]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAI3BA17MKpo_1bjkFH5wX1qmhW7FfexYPrFUKUOWlPwn6tlhziQrxXe4ysa3yyV4ll-7GjYjLX3np8WTgrm7SZvb5FVUlmeSK2naeKAasgkJEr7k5G6qBxhD8HLQ9LW-8hyq8LZSgEKJipluz0VFvSCavezG63ZbJ4=)[[10]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAL4h1eg_xU7z9SsgGdOEKHfYfhb1lTIeNW5VIv3V9tjonzP1xFlReHnWUOdiuof07adRUFx1QhBVOHBSHxi0v0KO97gdMqA4Vorfj37kZNU-NL72xgdIdGTyLI1paNP1z08MfiKdrJ9zJjVbUgtE-9ga4UEVZBj4dO0zJW7tpGkfNul).

*   **Early Life:** The Great Depression instilled financial prudence [[89]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAI3BA17MKpo_1bjkFH5wX1qmhW7FfexYPrFUKUOWlPwn6tlhziQrxXe4ysa3yyV4ll-7GjYjLX3np8WTgrm7SZvb5FVUlmeSK2naeKAasgkJEr7k5G6qBxhD8HLQ9LW-8hyq8LZSgEKJipluz0VFvSCavezG63ZbJ4=).
*   **World War II:** Served in the U.S. Army [[8]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAKx-ZCkraECpw2zpP3qVl6zL_kCwoSRIIQms84mnJ3E49BeG-kOeopfxzDFZ40PiUAEn1cR5ZqNJ9j0Sby6BQSF68aP5at43eEUVsycOsxUjuZjKY0qNb0jonsJRHBaOY5t9QZqnZLEZ7YtQ1VrvJs55mRIbyoN4c_Ki4gsNpBGfKt8z43S)[[10]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAL4h1eg_xU7z9SsgGdOEKHfYfhb1lTIeNW5VIv3V9tjonzP1xFlReHnWUOdiuof07adRUFx1QhBVOHBSHxi0v0KO97gdMqA4Vorfj37kZNU-NL72xgdIdGTyLI1paNP1z08MfiKdrJ9zJjVbUgtE-9ga4UEVZBj4dO0zJW7tpGkfNul).
*   **Benjamin Franklin:** A lifelong hero, inspiring determination [[8]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAKx-ZCkraECpw2zpP3qVl6zL_kCwoSRIIQms84mnJ3E49BeG-kOeopfxzDFZ40PiUAEn1cR5ZqNJ9j0Sby6BQSF68aP5at43eEUVsycOsxUjuZjKY0qNb0jonsJRHBaOY5t9QZqnZLEZ7YtQ1VrvJs55mRIbyoN4c_Ki4gsNpBGfKt8z43S).
*   **Warren Buffett:** Meeting in 1959 led Munger to investment management [[8]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAKx-ZCkraECpw2zpP3qVl6zL_kCwoSRIIQms84mnJ3E49BeG-kOeopfxzDFZ40PiUAEn1cR5ZqNJ9j0Sby6BQSF68aP5at43eEUVsycOsxUjuZjKY0qNb0jonsJRHBaOY5t9QZqnZLEZ7YtQ1VrvJs55mRIbyoN4c_Ki4gsNpBGfKt8z43S)[[9]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAKXLueM8ZuT3A8vgRpHvN-PQexxg3Z1hpcB2BeeVLkmF5l6VWceGZ7cLE1xJ7fXMJ2S4YYYgcQUsJHPt4bKnbNmbOQuykdO62WHXejx96OuSLkxmb-TmiOjvf_Fjq5gF2YjRCOGBgTfxt79Tg-NSqtdvxjKYiVCixTdwmSzhALvj180UA==).
*   **Benjamin Graham:** Learned value investing but evolved beyond it [[7]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAKu-mA-5Qb9GXZnlbXXj_H_K0sBkvQl6SbqaHcj3ht82phjX3gcxSL38qNa32YY4DaKGCrpJFOKSJXl1upsgEsSotWEJieEMRMov2PPeBL7Qj015rU8moyUsCutr3hBZJAfnlv1_6p7HSF4SjRw2_z50wYMmsICu3HrvT79cLCrfhLE8w==)[[8]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAKx-ZCkraECpw2zpP3qVl6zL_kCwoSRIIQms84mnJ3E49BeG-kOeopfxzDFZ40PiUAEn1cR5ZqNJ9j0Sby6BQSF68aP5at43eEUVsycOsxUjuZjKY0qNb0jonsJRHBaOY5t9QZqnZLEZ7YtQ1VrvJs55mRIbyoN4c_Ki4gsNpBGfKt8z43S).
*   **Historical Events:** The dot-com bubble and the 2008 financial crisis tested and validated his approach [[89]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAI3BA17MKpo_1bjkFH5wX1qmhW7FfexYPrFUKUOWlPwn6tlhziQrxXe4ysa3yyV4ll-7GjYjLX3np8WTgrm7SZvb5FVUlmeSK2naeKAasgkJEr7k5G6qBxhD8HLQ9LW-8hyq8LZSgEKJipluz0VFvSCavezG63ZbJ4=).
*   **Personal Experiences:** Personal tragedies shaped his views [[8]](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AWQVqAKx-ZCkraECpw2zpP3qVl6zL_kCwoSRIIQms84mnJ3E49BeG-kOeopfxzDFZ40PiUAEn1cR5ZqNJ9j0Sby6BQSF68aP5at43eEUVsycOsxUjuZjKY0qNb0jonsJRHBaOY5t9QZqnZLEZ7YtQ1VrvJs55mRIbyoN4c_Ki4gsNpBGfKt8z43S).

### **Summary**

Charlie Munger's investment philosophy is a powerful blend of value investing principles, a deep understanding of human psychology, and a multidisciplinary approach to thinking
